# Kiwi Gym Workout Log

Workout #724

30 seconds Monkey Walks +
30 seconds Alternating Superman Punches +
30 seconds Double Fist Reach-Ups +
30 seconds V-Ups

3 Rounds

Then:

15x Front Squat +
15x Glute Bridge Chest Press +
15x Bent Over Row - Palms Forward

3 Rounds

Then:

15 per side Split Squat to Shoulder Press +
15x Push-Ups +
15 per side Alternating Core Row +
15x Bicep Curl to Shoulder Press

3 Rounds

Then:

Walking Lunges - 100 meters

---

Workout #723

30 seconds Grapplers +
30 seconds per side Jane Fonda's +
30 seconds Lizard Kicks +
30 seconds Harvesters

3 Rounds

Then:

15x RDL +
20x Push-Up with Twist +
15x Bent Over Row - Palms Forward

3 Rounds

Then:

15x Squat to Shoulder Press +
15x Frog Jumps +
15x Gorillas +
15x Lat. Row

3 Rounds

Then:

Goblet Run - 400 meters

---

Workout #722

30 seconds Half Caterpillars +

15x Gorillas

3 Rounds

Then:

Run - 200 meters

4 Rounds / leave every 3 minutes

Workout #719

30 seconds per side each direction Dirty Dog Leg Circles +
30 seconds Grapplers +
10 per side Alternating Superman Punches +
10 per side Weighted Window Wipers

3 Rounds

Then:

10x Goblet Squat +
30 seconds Bear Crawl

3 Rounds

Then:

10x Glute Bridge Chest Press +
30 seconds Bear Walkout

3 Rounds

Then:

10x Bent Over Row - Palms Forward +
30 seconds Grapplers

3 Rounds

Then:

10 per side Alternating Core Row +
10x Squat to Shoulder Press +
10x Bicep Curl to Shoulder Press +
20x Gorillas

10 minutes

Then:

Run - 400 meters

3 Rounds / leave every 4 minutes

Workout #399

10 per side Jane Fonda's +
10x V-Ups +
10 per side Grapplers

8 minutes

Then:

5 per side Single Leg Caterpillars +
10 per side Weighted Window Wipers

3 Rounds

Then:

Glute Bridge Chest Press +
Alternating Core Row +
Frog Jumps +
Rear Delt Flys +
Bear Crawl 500 total reps To complete this block you are to do as many reps of each exercise as you can before you pause or need a break. When that happens, move onto the next exercise and continue the running rep count. So if you complete 16 reps of the first exercise, you start the next exercise on 17 reps. Keep a running count of reps, don't start from zero each time and then try and add them up after the set.

Then:

Run - 1000 meters

---
